atha sanatkumārasaṃhitā prārabhyate ||
sanatkumāra saṃhitāyāṃ
śrīgaṇeśāyanamaḥ ||
athasanatkumārasaṃhitāprārabhyate ||
prapadyedevamī śānaṃsarvajñamaparājitam ||
saṃbhavaṃsarvabhūtānāmanādiviśvatomukham || 1 ||
vedādauyaḥsvaraḥproktaoṃkārākhyomaheśvaraḥ ||
sṛjate sarvabhūtānipaṃcabhūtaiḥsadāśivaḥ || 2 ||
sāṃkhyānāṃparamaṃyogaṃvrataiḥpāśupataistathā ||
sarvajñānasyakartāramādidevamumāpatim || 3 ||
sṛjate bhagavāndevomūrtitrayavikārajān ||
rakṣārtha sarvajaṃtūnāṃtridhātmānaṃ sṛjatyajaḥ || 4 ||
sasaṃjñayātubhagavānekaevama heśvaraḥ ||
trailokyahitakārārthīnityamuktaḥ śivo'vyayaḥ || 5 ||
prajvalaṃtaṃ mahāśūlaṃghorarūpaṃ mahāśanim ||
nānākrīḍanakairdevaḥ krīḍateyogamāyayā || 6 ||
dayitārdhavapuḥrutvānṛtyāraṃbhesthitoharaḥ ||
jagatsthitiṃcakurute lokasyā'nugrahaṃśivaḥ || 7 ||
tasya ciṃtāprabhāvenanatasyaviditaṃjagat ||
tadbhaktyāsaṃpravakṣyāmipurāṇaṃśivabhāṣitam || 8 ||
naimiṣasthāśramapadepuṇye pūrvamayodi te ||
parāśarasyadāyādaḥśrīmānsatyavatīsutaḥ || 9 ||
brahmarṣiḥ sacadharmātmākālayogavidāṃvaraḥ ||
gururlokasyadharmātmāvala cārītaponidhiḥ || 10 ||
ṛṣisaṃdhaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śrutairivapitāmahaḥ ||
bhārateśatasāhakhyāṃsaṃhitāyāṃkavīśvaraḥ || 11 ||
devoyotra jhaṇāproktaṃbahmaiva punaranyathā ||
caturdhāvyasyamatimāniiśaṣyāṃścā'dhyāpayatpṛthak || 12 ||
teṣāṃsukhopaviṣṭānāṃ kathāṃ kathayatāṃ parām ||
tatra cādhyātmadharmātmābrahmaṇastanayaḥ śubhaḥ || 13 ||
anugrahārthamṭaṣīṇāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtavānṛṣiḥ |
sadadarśasukhāsīnān brahmarṣīnamitaujasaḥ || 14 ||
pratijagrāhavidhivatsacāpimunipuṃgavaḥ ||
arghyamācamanīyaṃcateṣāṃdattaṃcadharmavit || 15 ||
tataḥ saṃpūjayāmāsavalapīnsaṃśi tavratān ||
vidhinābrahmaṇoktenabhagavānbrahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ || 16 ||
anujñātaścataiḥ sarvairupaviṣṭaḥ kuśāsane ||
pṛṣṭastuṛṣibhistatratra hmaputromahāmuniḥ || 17 ||
liṃgārcana vidhiṃ caiva devadevasyapūjanam ||
prāsādasyacayatpuṇyaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ || 18 ||
saṃvatsa rasyayatpūjaśivasyaparamaṃphalam ||
āvartakavidhicaivapunarāvartakatathā || 19 ||
mūrtīnāṃtu vibhāgasya maṃtrasya paramaṃvidhim ||
sthānānityaṣṭāvasyāpirudrasyatumahātmanaḥ || 20 ||
upaviṣṭaistu bhagavān yogīśobrahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ||
tapoveṣānurūpeṣu āsaneṣu yathāyatham || 21 ||
sanatkumārastaiḥ sarvairdivākarasamaprabhaiḥ ||
virājatyadhikaṃbrahmātaiśvavahmarṣibhiḥ sadā || 22 ||
satāṃmadhyeca dharmātmā bhagavāntsūkṣmayogavit ||
kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve ṛṣayastamathābruvan || 23 ||
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃ hitāyāṃprathamo'dhyāyaḥ || 1 ||
ṛṣayaūcuḥ ||
tvattaśraśrotumicchā mastvatra puṇyaṃ sanātanam ||
śaivaṃ purāṇaṃde vasyayadvṛttaṃtadbravīhinaḥ || 1 ||
nahikiṃcidaviditaṃ trailokyajñānavānasi ||
sa evamuktastairvitrairbrahmaputro'vavīttadā || 2 ||
sana tkumāra uvāca ||
śaivaṃ purāṇaṃbhavataḥ śṛṇudhvaṃdvijasattamāḥ ||
mayocyamānaṃ tattvena devagulyaṃ sanātanam || 3 ||
yacchrutvā nirmalāḥ saṃtastaccittāstatparāyaṇāḥ ||
bhavaṃtibhāvitātmānaḥ kṛtakṛtyāviśeṣataḥ || 4 ||
dhanyaṃyaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ svargyamārogyamevaca ||
sva rgakāmapradaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam || 5 ||
itiśrīśivamahāpurāṇīyasanatkumārasaṃhitāvivṛtau prathamodhyāyaḥ || 1 ||
11 & 11 oṃoṃnamaḥ śivāya athadvitīyeṛṣibhiḥ pṛṣṭobrahmasutobravīt ||
kīrtanaṃ devadevasya harasya paramaṃśivam ||
pāvanaṃśraddadhānānāmihaloke paratraca || 6 ||
prakṛtyārthādhikāreṇapradhānapurupeśvara m ||
kīrtayiṣyāmivoviprāḥ purāṇaṃśivabhāpitam || 7 ||
śrutaṃpurāmayāvyāsāddevadevasya dhīmataḥ ||
yadahaṃtatpravakṣyāmiyathā pūrvaśrutaṃ mayā || 8 ||
naśakyaṃ vistarādvaktumapi varṣaśatairapi ||
saṃkṣepāccaivavakṣyāmipṛthivyādiyathātathā || 9 ||
brahmaviṣṇusa mutpatti saṃvādaharibrahmaṇoḥ ||
saptadvīpasyacākhyānaṃvarṣāṇāṃcatathaivaca || 10 ||
adhastādatha cordhvaṃ cacaṃdrasūryagrahādica ||
sana tkumāravikāṃtaṃrudrasyavihitaṃkṛtam || 11 ||
ārādhitaṃ mahādevaṃbrahmaṇastanayenatu ||
varadānenasaṃbaṃdhomuniśiṣyasamāgamaḥ || 12 ||
bhavanaṃmeruśṛṃgasyabrahmaviṣṇumaheśvarān ||
vibhīṣaṇasya saṃvādaṃ rudrasya ca mahātmanaḥ || 13 ||
sarvatīrthaphalaṃpuṇyaṃśiva liṃgasyapūjanam ||
śivaliṃgasamutpattiliṃgepralayamevaca || 14 ||
liṃgārcanavidhiṃcaiva devasya pūjanaṃtathā ||
prāsādasya caya tpuṇyaṃmahādevasyadhīmataḥ || 15 ||
saṃvatsarasya yatsūkṣmaṃśivasya paramaṃ phalam ||
āvartanavidhicaiva punarāvartikaṃtathā || 16 ||
mūttīnāṃ pravibhāgena rudrasya paramaṃvidhim ||
sthānādijyaiṣṭhyamasyāpirūpasya tu mahātmanaḥ || 17 ||
śivasyaparamaṃdivyaṃ tattvaṃca paramātmanaḥ ||
devasyacapavitraṃtugutyaṃ caivatathāṣṭakaṃ || 18 ||
liṃgodbhavaṃ ca devasya brahmaviṣṇvośvamohanaṃ ||
liṃgasaṃsthāpanepuṇyaṃ puṣpadānasya yatphalam || 19 ||
dhūpasyaca vidhiṃcaivamāsānāṃcaparaṃphalam ||
anāśakavidhiṃcaiva dānasyavidhimuttamam || 20 ||
yathādvādaśajyotirligādīnām || 17 ||
gusaṃrahasyam || 18 ||
anāśakavidhimupavāsavidhi || 20 ||
caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāṃ vidhāne vihitephalam ||
nāmāṣṭamīvidhānaṃ catathāvailakṣaṇāṣṭamīm || 21 ||
vibhūtiṃdevadevasyaīśvara syacadhīmataḥ ||
śaucācāravidhiproktaṃyogasya vidhimuttamam || 22 ||
yoganāḍyāstathākhyānaṃmayāproktaṃ purātanam ||
avimu ktasyamāhātmyaṃtathācoṃkāravarṇanam || 23 ||
yajñeśvarasyamāhātmyaṃta thātīrthānuvarṇanam ||
bhagavadārādhanaṃnaṃdestathānaṃyabhiṣe canam || 24 ||
nīlakaṃṭhasya māhātmyaṃtripurasya tathāvadhaḥ ||
vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃvidhānaṃcaivatasyaca || 25 ||
sarvadharmaṃ hara syā pimahādevasya kīrttanam ||
jñānapraśaṃsanaṃcaiva mokṣaṃ paramasaṃpadam || 26 ||
itisaṃgrahaṇaṃ proktaṃtathāvastuparigraham ||
idānīṃvi staraṃcitraṃvibhāgaṃrūpamaiśvaram || 27 ||
āsīttamomayaṃ sarvamaprajñātamalakṣaṇam ||
tatraraktomahāyogīrudraḥ paramakāraṇam || 28 ||
ātmanāsarvamātmānaṃsaṃciṃtyabhagavānharaḥ ||
manaḥsaṃsṛjate pūrva mahaṃkāraṃtupṛṣṭhataḥ || 29 ||
ahaṃkārātprajātānimahā bhūtānipaṃcaca ||
aṣṭauprakṛtayaḥ proktāvikārāścaiva ṣoḍaśa || 30 ||
śabdaḥsparśaśvarūpaṃcarasogaṃdhastathaiva ca ||
prāṇopānaḥ samā naśvaudānovyānaevaca || 31 ||
satvaṃrajastamaścaiva guṇāḥproktāstutetrayaḥ ||
tasmādbhagavato brahmātasmādviṣṇurajāyata || 32 ||
brahmaviṣṇvormohanārthatataḥ saṃbhavatimahān ||
aśarīromahādevo anutpattirayonijaḥ || 33 ||
vyāmohayitvātatsarva tejasā mohitaṃjagat ||
tasmātparataraṃnāsti nāstitasmātparaṃśivam || 34 ||
brahmāviṣṇuśrvadvāvetāvudbhūtauśaṃkarā ttutau ||
kalpekalpetu tatsarvaissṛjato mohayan jagat || 35 ||
tapasāharatecaivanānābhūtānisarvaśaḥ ||
ekasaptatiyugānyevamanvaṃtaraitismṛtaḥ || 36 ||
caturdaśatutānyevakalpa me kaṃvidhīya te ||
dinaikaṃbrahmaṇaḥ proktaṃniśākalpastathācyate || 37 ||
evaṃmāsaṃcavarṣacatathāvarṣaśataṃdvijāḥ ||
evamādiparārdhītoharasyani miṣaḥsmṛtaḥ || 38 ||
brahmādistaṃbaparyaṃtaṃnimiṣaśca maheśvaraḥ |
nimiṣaṃjīvitaṃ sarva caṃdrādīnāṃ grahaiḥ saha || 39 ||
nimiṣārdhapra suptasyadaivatairṛṣibhiḥ saha ||
evaṃviśvamidaṃ sarvasaptalokaṃcarācaram || 40 ||
bhūrloko'thabhuvarlokaḥ svarlokaśca mahastathā ||
janastapaśvasatyaṃ catrahmalokaśvasaptamaḥ || 41 ||
pātālaṃsutalaṃtālaṃvitalaṃtalamevaca ||
paṃcamaṃviddhipātālaṃrukmasauvarṇikaṃ smṛtam || 42 ||
saptamaṃśarkarābhūmiraṣṭamaṃvijayaṃsmṛtam ||
eteṣudharma prakhyātā aṣṭaupātālavāsinaḥ || 43 ||
eṣāmādaucama dhyeca aṃte rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||
evaṃ prakurute lokānkrīḍārthaṃ tumaheśvaraḥ || 44 ||
brahmalokaparīmāṇagatirūrdhvavivarṇitā ||
pṛthi vīcāṃtarikṣaṃcadiśaśrvavidiśastathā || 45 ||
samuccayaṃgirīṇāṃca anukramaṇasaṃkhyayā ||
samudrāṇāṃcavistāraṃpramāṇaṃcata thāśṭaṇu || 46 ||
sthāvarāṇāṃcarāṇāṃ cadevānāṃca divaukasām ||
catuṣpādadvipādānāṃ dhārmikān karmamokṣakān || 47 ||
sa hasraguṇamākhyātaṃsthāvarāṇāṃprakīrtitam ||
sahasaṃpādahīnāśvaityāha bhagavāśivaḥ || 48 ||
maheśvaraḥ parasteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃdeva mānuṣāt ||
evaṃ saṃkhyā'trasaṃkhyātāsarvajñenasvayaṃbhuvā || 49 ||
eṣāṃmāheśvaraṃ jñānaṃbhaktimaṃtraiḥ prakīrtitam ||
sarvakarmasuvartta teyatastuśivamavyayam || 50 ||
ekaṃjñānaṃnamasyaṃtiabhūtaṃbhūtasaṃjñakam ||
nirguṇaṃnirmalaṃjñānaṃśaṃkareṇapracoditam || 51 ||
ṛṣīṇāṃ śrotukāmānāṃ bhaktā nāṃcadṛḍhavrata ||
śrāvitaṃjñāna sarvasvaṃ purāṇeṣucagīyate || 52 ||
tatojñānaṃparaṃ śreṣṭha proktamīśena dhīmatā ||
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya sarvavarṇeviśeṣataḥ || 53 ||
yathāsaṃbhavatijñānaṃtathāīśaḥpravartate ||
ahamādiśvamadhyaṃca ahaṃcatecasaṃsthitaḥ || 54 ||
krīḍā rthamīhatevyāsa utpannamatiravyayaḥ ||
ekaevaśivastatratasmātkāloyathā'bhavat || 55 ||
kālaevahitatsarvaṃ kālādanyona vidyate ||
tataḥkālohibhagavān sobhidhyāyaśivājñayā || 56 ||
sṛṣṭituprathamaṃ kurvanprakṛtināmanāmataḥ ||
tasmādbrahmāpraka tyāstu utpannaḥsahaviṣṇunā || 57 ||
tataḥ svamukhatobrahmābrāhmaṇāntsa makalpayat ||
pādahīnānkṣaciyāṃśvatasmāddhīnāṃstu vaiśya kān || 58 ||
caturthapādahīnāṃśva ācāraiśvavahiṣkṛtān ||
samudrānparvatāntrahmācodyamānaḥ śivenavai || 59 ||
pṛthivīṃcāṃ ‘tarikṣaṃcadiśaścaiva makalpayat ||

vidyutstanitanirghoṣarohiteṃdradhanūṃṣica || 61 ||
ulkānipātaṃ ketuṃ ca jyotiṣāṃpatanānyapi ||

vyāsauvā ca ||

parimāṇaṃcasaṃkhyāṃcadvīpapravaramevaca ||

sahasraṃśa tamekaṃcayojanānāṃsamucchritaḥ ||
tasyajaṃbūphalarasaścāmṛtasvādurucyate || 25 ||

saptavargāḥprasaṃkhyātāḥ samaiva kulaparvatāḥ ||

dakṣiṇenavisaṃ khyātamilāvattaṃprakīrtitam ||
uttaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃcaiva iṃdradhanvākṛtiryathā || 29 ||
